/* LOCODES_SMALL_HEADER 30/05/2025
 
 $$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$
 $   LOCODES_SMALL_HEADER.txt - header   $
 $$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$$
 
 by W.B. Yates    
 Copyright (c) W.B. Yates. All rights reserved. 
 
 History:

 A subset of 26857 UN/LOCODE codes with status AM, AA, AC, AI, AF or AS. Ordered alphabetically.
 The other codes (with status RL, RQ, RN, QQ) that occur here have been included from City.
 

 
 UN/LOCODE Composition
 ----------------------------------------------------------------
 Status | Number of Codes | Number with Coordinates
 ----------------------------------------------------------------
 AM     |     587         |       586
 AA     |    9349         |      8940
 AC     |     658         |       402
 AI     |    7480         |      2486
 AF     |    7631         |      2839
 AS     |     905         |       484
 RL     |     159         |       154
 RQ     |      75         |        75
 RN     |       7         |         7
 QQ     |       4         |         4
 NONE   |       1         |         0
 ----------------------------------------------------------------
        |   26857         |     15977
 ----------------------------------------------------------------
 Approx 60% of the codes have coordinates.

*/
